programs.nim-moe

Moe: A command line based editor inspired by vi/vim. Written in Nim.

type

submodule

example

{
  programs.nim-moe = {
    Standard = {
      theme = "light";
    };
  };
}

default

{
  programs.nim-moe = {};
}

programs.nim-moe.AutoBackup

AutoBackup configuration

type

submodule

example

{
  programs.nim-moe.AutoBackup = {};
}

default

{
  programs.nim-moe.AutoBackup = {};
}

programs.nim-moe.AutoBackup.enable

Enable/Disable automatic backups

null is true

type

null or boolean

example

{
  programs.nim-moe.AutoBackup.enable = false;
}

default

{
  programs.nim-moe.AutoBackup.enable = null;
}

programs.nim-moe.AutoBackup.backupDir

Directory to save backup files If not set, it will be saved in .hisotry in the same directory as the original file.

type

null or string

example

{
  programs.nim-moe.AutoBackup.backupDir = "~/project";
}

default

{
  programs.nim-moe.AutoBackup.backupDir = null;
}

programs.nim-moe.AutoBackup.dirToExclude

Exclude settings for where you don't want to produce automatic backups

type

null or list of string

example

{
  programs.nim-moe.AutoBackup.dirToExclude = [
    "/etc"
  ];
}

default

{
  programs.nim-moe.AutoBackup.dirToExclude = null;
}

programs.nim-moe.AutoBackup.idleTime

Start backup when there is no operation for the set number of seconds

null is 10

type

null or positive integer, meaning >0

example

{
  programs.nim-moe.AutoBackup.idleTime = 8;
}

default

{
  programs.nim-moe.AutoBackup.idleTime = null;
}

programs.nim-moe.AutoBackup.interval

Backup interval

null is 5

type

null or positive integer, meaning >0

example

{
  programs.nim-moe.AutoBackup.interval = 5;
}

default

{
  programs.nim-moe.AutoBackup.interval = null;
}

programs.spacevim.enable

Whether to enable hahahhahah spacevim.

type

boolean

example

{
  programs.spacevim.enable = true;
}

default

{
  programs.spacevim.enable = false;
}

programs.spacevim.config

SpaceVim configuration

type

YAML value

default

{
  programs.spacevim.config = {
    layers = {
      autocomplete = {
        auto-completion-return-key-behavior = "complete";
      };
    };
  };
}

services.espanso.enable

Whether to enable Espanso: cross platform text expander in Rust.

type

boolean

example

{
  services.espanso.enable = true;
}

default

{
  services.espanso.enable = false;
}

services.espanso.config

Espanso configuration

type

YAML value

default

{
  services.espanso.config = {
    matches = [
      {
        replace = "{{mydate}}";
        trigger = ":date";
        vars = [
          {
            name = "mydate";
            params = {
              format = "%m/%d/%Y";
            };
            type = "date";
          }
        ];
      }
      {
        replace = "Hi there!";
        trigger = ":espanso";
      }
      {
        replace = "{{output}}";
        trigger = ":shell";
        vars = [
          {
            name = "output";
            params = {
              cmd = "echo Hello from your shell";
            };
            type = "shell";
          }
        ];
      }
    ];
  };
}
